                        <div data-reactid="657">
                         Your home away from home in Mt. Park includes 2 bedrooms, a beautiful kitchen &amp; living area, &amp; your own bathroom. The home is in a quiet, safe &amp; friendly neighborhood with scenic hiking trails just out the back door. There are several shopping complexes less than 2 miles away. Amenities include high end linens, HD cable pkg, broadcast networks, Netflix &amp; Amazon Prime. 5 min off of I-5 freeway, approx. 15 min to downtown Portland, 10 min to Lewis &amp; Clark college.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="658">
                         We are conveniently located just 15 minutes from downtown Portland (can be longer during rush hour) and only 5 minutes from freeway access. As we are centrally located, Mt. Hood skiing, the Columbia River gorge and the Willamette Valley wine country are all only about one hour away - just in different directions! The central location and great neighborhood is a huge draw as to why people want to live here! The suite is a great setting for both business &amp; leisure travelers with high speed WiFi. Relax and enjoy a private secluded wing in the lower level of our home. (We live on the upper level.) The space includes two bedrooms, a private bath and a beautiful kitchen with granite counter tops, cherry cabinets, hardwood floors, and stainless appliances (dishwasher, gas range, and full size refrigerator and lots of counter space!) The great room is voice controlled with digital lighting so if you want to turn on any of the lights, you just speak the command! "Turn on Kitchen lights, 50%!" The good old fashioned light switches work as well! We request that our guests sleep on the beds provided (not on the sofa). If a third bed is desired (floor mattress or camping pad), there is an additional $25 per night fee. The upper level of our home is air-conditioned, but the lower level (where your suite is located) is not air-conditioned. After staying with us (even on a super hot day), you will see why it is not needed! The property is in a safe, quiet neighborhood, yet centrally located in the greater Portland area.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="659">
                         In our upscale neighborhood you can walk through the forest on about 15 miles of paved trails surrounding our home. The tree lined street is quiet and peaceful. New Seasons, a grocery store with an abundance of organic food choices, is about 1 mile away. Other stores/shops include Starbucks, a nail salon, Columbia Outlet store, etc. Kruse Village, about 5 minutes away in the Meadows Road financial services center of Lake Oswego, is a restaurant hub spanning 5 acres with many choices to delight your palette. And just down Meadows Road from there is Hunan Pearl, our favorite Chinese restaurant!

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1365">
                       <div data-reactid="1366">
                        <div data-reactid="1367">
                         Located in beautiful Mt Park, a great opportunity to have a comfortable, quiet, room or entire home, especially good if you're contemplating a move to the Portland area - three minutes to I-5/217, ten minutes to downtown Portland and Lake Oswego.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1368">
                         You can have the guest room or for $50 more, opt to have the entire home, spacious, quiet and comfortable, with a private backyard in beautiful Mountain Park, Lake Oswego, (voted one of the top 10 places to retire in the USA). There is a recreation center with olympic size pool for lap swim, weight room, free exercise classes and tennis courts, two minutes from the major freeways and 10 minutes from downtown Portland - convenient to outdoor activities, 17 miles of walking trails and parks, indigenous wildlife as well as the Lake, great shops and restaurants. I have travelled in Europe and speak minimum French, Italian and Spanish. There is a master bedroom for two with vaulted ceilings, a queen bed and private bath and a smaller bedroom with a single bed and private bath. There's wi-fi, Apple TV, lots of CD's and DVD's, all in surround sound, no cable TV. Parking is available in the driveway. You will need a car.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1369">
                         It's safe and quiet, easy to walk and hike, has a small town ambiance but 10-15 minutes to downtown Portland.
                        </div>

                        <div data-reactid="1758">
                         Home away from home. If you're here for work, visiting, need a temporary place to stay, this is the place for you. It is 600 Sq ft, comes with a kitchen, bathroom, and bedroom. You have your own private space on the first floor of the main house.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1759">
                         This space is perfect for those who need their privacy, want a semblance of home, and doesn't want to stay at a hotel. It's got everything you need to make your stay comfortable. The kitchen comes fully stocked with appliances to make your own meals and coffee. Situated in a quiet neighborhood with beautiful views of the valley. We are close to major freeways- hwy 217, I-5, and I-205, near shopping centers, and an hour to two away from the beach and Mt. Hood.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1760">
                         It is nice and quiet. We live on top of Bull Mountain, so you can see a beautiful view of the valley from the front porch and on a sunny day you can see Mt. Hood. During sunny days the neighborhood kids will be out and you can hear kids playing and laughing. The neighbors are friendly. It's a great neighborhood.

                        <div data-reactid="1889">
                         We invite you to stay in our private 2-bedroom, 1-bath, apartment. This gorgeous, family-friendly residence has its own entrance and is completely independent from the rest of our home. Great amenities make it feel like your home away from home.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1890">
                         LOCATION: Our home is located in Hillshire Estates, one of the most beautiful hilltop communities in SW Portland. The house itself is a two-story traditional farmhouse complete with a wrap-around porch and rocking chairs. It backs onto a green space with 100 foot Douglas fir trees and a meandering creek. This beautiful location on the edge of Portland's Urban Growth Boundary provides easy access to all the best downtown Portland has to offer while placing you just a short distance from the Willamette Valley’s vineyards and the berry farms that dot the surrounding hillsides. TRAVEL TIMES: 1.5 hours to the Oregon Coast 1.5 hours to Mt. Hood 45 minutes to Multnomah Falls 30 minutes to the Airport 20 minutes to Downtown 20 minutes to Wine Country 15 minutes to the Oregon Zoo 10 minutes to local hiking trails 5 minutes to local farms and markets BEDROOMS: Our guest suite offers sleeping for five. The master bedroom features a queen bed with high thread count sheets, a walk in closet with a full capacity, stacked washer and dryer. The second bedroom is located upstairs off the private foyer and has a bunk bed that will comfortably sleep two adults. The living room sofa converts into a twin bed for a fifth person, if needed. KITCHEN: A well-appointed kitchen with slab granite countertops, stainless steel appliances, and five burner professional grade stove is perfect for preparing all of your gourmet meals. Pots, pans, and a plethora of kitchen tools and appliances are also provided. Help yourself to fresh herbs growing off your private patio. LIVING ROOM: The breakfast bar overlooks the living room complete with a gas-burning fireplace, large comfy chairs, and picture windows that bring the outside in. The unit is complete with wireless internet, HD flat-screen TV, and a Blu-ray DVD player. Cable, Netflix and Hulu are also provided. BATHROOM: The four piece washroom features granite countertops and stainless steel fixtures. Plush towels, soap, and shampoo are provided for all our guests. GARDEN: A private patio features a comfortable bistro set perfect for dining alfresco. The patio also has a gas barbecue for grilling out with the family. A vegetable garden with seasonal fruits and vegetables is available to our guests. We also have four chickens that provide fresh eggs daily. You are welcome to check the coop and see if there are any fresh eggs available for your breakfast. WE INVITE YOU TO COME AND VISIT: Our desire is to create a home away from home with everything you would need for an extended business trip or a holiday with the kids. You will find all kinds of resources and guidebooks to Portland and the surrounding areas. Whether you spend your time exploring our amazing city or want a quiet retreat to rest and relax, our space is designed to accommodate both. We may or may not see you but, either way, we hope you will have a wonderful time staying in our guest apartment.
                        </div>
